context errors (DeadlineExceeded, Canceled) to gRPC errors\\n\\n**Error Translation Pattern:**\\netcd translates gRPC errors to HTTP at multiple layers:\\n1. translation\\n\\n### Grafana/Grafana\\n\\n**Error Creation Pattern:**\\nGrafana creates gRPC errors in service handlers:\\n- **pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go**: RBAC service returns Pattern:**\\nGrafana translates gRPC status codes to backend response status codes:\\n1. **pkg/tsdb/influxdb/fsql/fsql.go**: The `Query()` function uses `status.FromError()` to extract gRPC status, then switches on the code (codes.InvalidArgument, codes.PermissionDenied, codes.NotFound, codes.Unavailable, codes.Unauthenticated) to construct `backend.ErrDataResponseWithSource()` responses with appropriate backend status codes\\n2. **pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go**: The `handleGrpcStatusError()` function sets error source context (ErrorSourceDownstream or ErrorSourcePlugin) and returns plugin-specific error wrappers. Also checks `status.Code(err) == codes.Unavailable` and `codes.Unimplemented` to determine plugin state\\n3. **pkg/tsdb/jaeger/grpc_client.go**: Similar pattern checking gRPC status codes and mapping to backend error sources\\n\\n### Cross-Repository Patterns\\n\\nAll three projects follow a consistent pattern:\\n1. **Error Creation**: Use `status.Error(codes.*, message)` to create typed gRPC errors\\n2. **Error Propagation**: Return gRPC errors through the call chain\\n3. **Error Translation**: Extract status with `status.FromError()` and switch on the code to map to target protocol (HTTP status codes for Kubernetes and etcd, backend response codes for Grafana)\\n4. **Centralization**: etcd stands out with its comprehensive centralized error definitions in rpctypes/error.go, whereas Kubernetes and Grafana create errors closer to where they're used\\n\\nThe key difference in propagation models:\\n- **Kubernetes**: Simple two-step conversion (gRPC → HTTP) with grpc-gateway providing the standard mapping\\n- **etcd**: Multi-layer approach with centralized error definitions and per-handler HTTP translation\\n- **Grafana**: Backend-aware translation that maps to plugin SDK response codes rather than raw HTTP status codes\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":4004,"cache_read_input_tokens":84662,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":4004},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"56c62e83-eeae-4d20-85e8-1330a9f34372","uuid":"19d8861f-c752-4535-9a7a-046f37189e0e"}

`togRPCError()` function providing fallback to `status.Error(codes.Unknown, err.Error())` for unmapped errors\\n- **client/v3/retry_interceptor.go**: The `contextErrToGRPCErr()` function converts context errors (DeadlineExceeded, Canceled) to gRPC errors\\n\\n**Error Translation Pattern:**\\netcd translates gRPC errors to HTTP at multiple layers:\\n1. **server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/interceptor.go**: Unary server interceptor validates capability flags and returns predefined gRPC errors\\n2. **server/etcdserver/api/etcdhttp/peer.go**: HTTP handler for peer operations checks error types and maps to HTTP status codes (e.g., `http.StatusNotFound`, `http.StatusPreconditionFailed`)\\n3. **server/lease/leasehttp/http.go**: HTTP lease handler checks `resp.StatusCode == http.StatusNotFound` and maps to `lease.ErrLeaseNotFound`\\n4. **server/etcdserver/api/v2error/error.go**: Legacy v2 error mapping provides direct error code to HTTP status translation\\n\\n### Grafana/Grafana\\n\\n**Error Creation Pattern:**\\nGrafana creates gRPC errors in service handlers:\\n- **pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go**: RBAC service returns `status.Error(codes.NotFound, \\\"unsupported resource\\\")` for missing resources and `status.Error(codes.NotFound, \\\"unsupported verb\\\")` for invalid verbs\\n\\n**Error Translation Pattern:**\\nGrafana translates gRPC status codes to backend response status codes:\\n1. **pkg/tsdb/influxdb/fsql/fsql.go**: The `Query()` function uses `status.FromError()` to extract gRPC status, then switches on the code (codes.InvalidArgument, codes.PermissionDenied, codes.NotFound, codes.Unavailable, codes.Unauthenticated) to construct `backend.ErrDataResponseWithSource()` responses with appropriate backend status codes\\n2. **pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go**: The `handleGrpcStatusError()` function sets error source context (ErrorSourceDownstream or ErrorSourcePlugin) and returns plugin-specific error wrappers. Also checks `status.Code(err) == codes.Unavailable` and `codes.Unimplemented` to determine plugin state\\n3. **pkg/tsdb/jaeger/grpc_client.go**: Similar pattern checking gRPC status codes and mapping to backend error sources\\n\\n### Cross-Repository Patterns\\n\\nAll three projects follow a consistent pattern:\\n1. **Error Creation**: Use `status.Error(codes.*, message)` to create typed gRPC errors\\n2. **Error Propagation**: Return gRPC errors through the call chain\\n3. **Error Translation**: Extract status with `status.FromError()` and switch on the code to map to target protocol (HTTP status codes for Kubernetes and etcd, backend response codes for Grafana)\\n4. **Centralization**: etcd stands out with its comprehensive centralized error definitions in rpctypes/error.go, whereas Kubernetes and Grafana create errors closer to where they're used\\n\\nThe key difference in propagation models:\\n- **Kubernetes**: Simple two-step conversion (gRPC → HTTP) with grpc-gateway providing the standard mapping\\n- **etcd**: Multi-layer approach with centralized error definitions and per-handler HTTP translation\\n- **Grafana**: Backend-aware translation that maps to plugin SDK response codes rather than raw HTTP status codes\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Key files include:\\n- **test/e2e/storage/drivers/csi-test/mock/service/controller.go**: Mock CSI controller creates errors like `status.Error(codes.NotFound, req.VolumeId)` for missing volumes\\n- **test/e2e/storage/drivers/csi-test/mock/service/node.go**: Mock CSI node service creates `status.Error(codes.Internal, msg)` for operational failures\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/errors/errors.go**: Helper that checks `s.Code() == codes.NotFound` to identify specific error types\\n\\n**Error Translation Pattern:**\\nKubernetes implements two-layer error translation to HTTP:\\n1. **staging/src/k8s.io/kubelet/pkg/cri/streaming/errors.go**: The `WriteError()` function extracts the gRPC status with `grpcstatus.FromError()`, then uses a switch statement to map codes to HTTP status codes (e.g., `codes.NotFound` → `http.StatusNotFound`, `codes.ResourceExhausted` → `http.StatusTooManyRequests`)\\n2. **vendor/github.com/grpc-ecosystem/grpc-gateway/v2/runtime/errors.go**: Comprehensive `HTTPStatusFromCode()` function provides standardized mappings for all gRPC codes (13+ cases) to HTTP status codes, with special handling for `codes.Canceled` (499) and defaults to `http.StatusInternalServerError`\\n\\n### etcd-io/etcd\\n\\n**Error Creation Pattern:**\\netcd uses a centralized error definition strategy with pre-constructed `status.Error` objects:\\n- **api/v3rpc/rpctypes/error.go**: Defines 70+ gRPC error constants with specific codes (codes.NotFound, codes.FailedPrecondition, codes.InvalidArgument, codes.Unavailable, etc.). Examples include `ErrGRPCMemberNotFound = status.Error(codes.NotFound, \\\"...\\\")`, `ErrGRPCLeaseNotFound = status.Error(codes.NotFound, \\\"...\\\")`, `ErrGRPCPermissionDenied = status.Error(codes.PermissionDenied, \\\"...\\\")`\\n- **server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go**: Contains `toGRPCErrorMap` that maps internal errors to these predefined gRPC errors, with the `togRPCError()` function providing fallback to `status.Error(codes.Unknown, err.Error())` for unmapped errors\\n- **client/v3/retry_interceptor.go**: The `contextErrToGRPCErr()` function converts context errors (DeadlineExceeded, Canceled) to gRPC errors\\n\\n**Error Translation Pattern:**\\netcd translates gRPC errors to HTTP at multiple layers:\\n1. **server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/interceptor.go**: Unary server interceptor validates capability flags and returns predefined gRPC errors\\n2. **server/etcdserver/api/etcdhttp/peer.go**: HTTP handler for peer operations checks error types and maps to HTTP status codes (e.g., `http.StatusNotFound`, `http.StatusPreconditionFailed`)\\n3. **server/lease/leasehttp/http.go**: HTTP lease handler checks `resp.StatusCode == http.StatusNotFound` and maps to `lease.ErrLeaseNotFound`\\n4. **server/etcdserver/api/v2error/error.go**: Legacy v2 error mapping provides direct error code to HTTP status translation\\n\\n### Grafana/Grafana\\n\\n**Error Creation Pattern:**\\nGrafana creates gRPC errors in service handlers:\\n- **pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go**: RBAC service returns `status.Error(codes.NotFound, \\\"unsupported resource\\\")` for missing resources and `status.Error(codes.NotFound, \\\"unsupported verb\\\")` for invalid verbs\\n\\n**Error Translation Pattern:**\\nGrafana translates gRPC status codes to backend response status codes:\\n1. **pkg/tsdb/influxdb/fsql/fsql.go**: The `Query()` function uses `status.FromError()` to extract gRPC status, then switches on the code (codes.InvalidArgument, codes.PermissionDenied, codes.NotFound, codes.Unavailable, codes.Unauthenticated) to construct `backend.ErrDataResponseWithSource()` responses with appropriate backend status codes\\n2. **pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go**: The `handleGrpcStatusError()` function sets error source context (ErrorSourceDownstream or ErrorSourcePlugin) and returns plugin-specific error wrappers. Also checks `status.Code(err) == codes.Unavailable` and `codes.Unimplemented` to determine plugin state\\n3. **pkg/tsdb/jaeger/grpc_client.go**: Similar pattern checking gRPC status codes and mapping to backend error sources\\n\\n### Cross-Repository Patterns\\n\\nAll three projects follow a consistent pattern:\\n1. **Error Creation**: Use `status.Error(codes.*, message)` to create typed gRPC errors\\n2. **Error Propagation**: Return gRPC errors through the call chain\\n3. **Error Translation**: Extract status with `status.FromError()` and switch on the code to map to target protocol (HTTP status codes for Kubernetes and etcd, backend response codes for Grafana)\\n4. **Centralization**: etcd stands out with its comprehensive centralized error definitions in rpctypes/error.go, whereas Kubernetes and Grafana create errors closer to where they're used\\n\\nThe key difference in propagation models:\\n- **Kubernetes**: Simple two-step conversion (gRPC → HTTP) with grpc-gateway providing the standard mapping\\n- **etcd**: Multi-layer approach with centralized error definitions and per-handler HTTP translation\\n- **Grafana**: Backend-aware translation that maps to plugin SDK response codes rather than raw HTTP status codes\"\n}\n","numLines":156,"startLine":1,"totalLines":156}}}
